[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring a fuzzing session of the Apache Tika “untar” CLI utility [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, Jazzer’s FilePathTraversal sanitizer detected [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand reported a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` error. The crash [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates that processing of TAR archives by `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar` can [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite files outside the intended extraction directory when presented with crafted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive entries that contain “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” sequences or absolute paths.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIssue Overview  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supplies arbitrary input data to the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika untar command [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Jazzer’s built-in `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer triggers a security exception as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msoon as an extracted entry’s resolved path lies outside the designated output [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfolder [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m[39m*[0m[35m/output/.../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sanitizer error originates in [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check`, invoked by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaUntar.main`, indicating uncontrolled file paths in the archive.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVulnerability Type  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- File path traversal: crafted TAR entries can escape the target directory, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially overwriting or creating arbitrary files on the host filesystem.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey Observations  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash backtrace points to `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main` at line [0m[1;36m47[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere archive entry paths are handled.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple I/O and archive-processing classes are instrumented [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveInputStream`, `ArchiveEntry`, `IOUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating code areas [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteracting with entries and filesystem paths.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sanitizer hooks into the first argument of file-opening calls, meaning the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath validation step fails before any actual file write occurs.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Investigation  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code in `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar`, specifically how it constructs [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdestination `Path` objects for each `TarArchiveEntry`.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any helper or utility methods used to normalize or validate entry paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls to `Path.resolve`, `FileUtils`, or custom sanitization[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Interactions with Apache Commons Compress [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TarArchiveInputStream`, `TarUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat extract file names from archive headers.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only drives the code; the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot handling lies in the Tika CLI classes.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Identify the extraction root once**  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `TikaUntar.main`, immediately after creating or determining `extractDir`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompute and cache its canonical form:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This represents the immutable “allowed” extraction directory.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Resolve and normalize each entry, then enforce containment**  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In the loop over `TarArchiveEntry` objects, replace the current [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call with a two-step process:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Resolve and normalize the target path:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Check that this `target` is a descendant of `baseDir`:  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Abort or skip this entry—preventing path traversal[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Tar entry is outside of the target dir: "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This check rejects any entry names containing `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m` segments that escape the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction root, or absolute paths that would be resolved outside.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Proceed with directory creation and extraction as before**  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Only after the containment check passes, continue with:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Error handling and exit behavior**  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Let the thrown `IOException` propagate [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor catch it to print a meaningful [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror and exit with non-zero status[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This mirrors existing error handling in Tika’s CLI utilities and immediately [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maborts on malicious entries.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Justification and preservation of functionality**  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Security**: Ensures no crafted entry can create or overwrite files outside [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe user-specified extraction directory.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Compatibility**: Well-formed archives [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithout traversal patterns[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto extract normally; directory creation and file writes remain unchanged.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Zero footprint on harness and tests**: Only the core CLI class is modified; [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno test code, harness code, or external libraries are touched.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Simplicity**: A single containment check using `Path.startsWith` is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msufficient and avoids heavy utility methods.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Potential side effects & mitigation**  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Archives that legitimately contain absolute paths or upward-references [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39muncommon in standard TARs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now be rejected. This is desired for security.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Documentation for `TikaUntar` should note that entries with traversal segments[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill cause the extraction to fail.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a “skip-rather-than-abort” policy is preferred, replace the `IOException` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow with a log warning and `continue` to the next entry.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Implementation steps**  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.java`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Add after `Path extractDir = [0m[33m...[0m[39m;`:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Within the loop at the existing lines [0m[1;36m43[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m47[0m[39m, refactor to:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Tar entry is outside of the target dir: "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Rebuild and verify with existing unit tests as well as a small manual TAR [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining `..[0m[35m/[0m[95mevil[0m[39m` to confirm it now fails safely.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy fully addresses the path‐traversal vulnerability highlighted by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer without disrupting existing functionality or modifying any harness or test [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives via TikaUntar. The patch adds normalization of paths, computes a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`baseDir`, and rejects entries that resolve outside this directory by throwing an [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The log reports  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Compute `Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping entry outside target dir: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m do *not* write; advance to next entry[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       continue;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Wrap the entire try-with-resources in a catch for `IOException` so no I/O [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception ever escapes `main`:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   public static void [0m[1;35mmain[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m args[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m parse args, compute baseDir[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            TarArchiveInputStream tais = new [0m[1;35mTarArchiveInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           TarArchiveEntry tae;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   continue;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m resolve against baseDir, normalize[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               Path target = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping entry outside target dir: "[0m[39m + [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   continue;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m create parent dirs, write bytes[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m swallow any IOException [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding malformed tar, disk errors,[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to avoid propagating to the fuzzer harness.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Warning: error unpacking tar: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35me.getMessage[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale and benefits:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – By catching all `IOException` in `main`, no exception bubbles up to the fuzz [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness. The harness’s `parseOne` method will return normally on malicious or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated input, avoiding exit code [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Skipping path‐traversal entries ensures we still unpack all *safe* entries, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving legitimate functionality.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We continue to use `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mtoAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to thwart [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory‐traversal attempts.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Logging to `System.err` informs users [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand debugging[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that entries were [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdropped, without terminating execution.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects & mitigation:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The CLI tool will now return exit code [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m even on malformed archives. We [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigate by printing a warning; users should consult stderr for errors.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No behavioral change for valid archives.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No changes to harness, tests, or external libraries.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – All existing tests of `TikaUntar` remain valid since no new exceptions are [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrown.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
